{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01999tUEbUnGnTquabr6kpLH","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_013Ld8d2ELMbcdqGJYnwovow","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Overview](#overview)\n2. [Core Types](#core-types)\n3. [Consumer Lifecycle](#consumer-lifecycle)\n4. [Subscription and Assignment](#subscription-and-assignment)\n5. [Polling and Data Fetching](#polling-and-data-fetching)\n6. [Offset Management](#offset-management)\n7. [Position and Seek Operations](#position-and-seek-operations)\n8. [Consumer Groups and Rebalancing](#consumer-groups-and-rebalancing)\n9. [Flow Control](#flow-control)\n10. [Metadata and Partition Information](#metadata-and-partition-information)\n11. [Multi-threaded Processing](#multi-threaded-processing)\n12. [Error Handling](#error-handling)\n13. [Configuration-Driven Behaviors](#configuration-driven-behaviors)\n14. [Common Patterns and Best Practices](#common-patterns-and-best-practices)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\n### Purpose\n\n`KafkaConsumer<K, V>` is the main client API for consuming records from Apache Kafka. It handles:\n- Connection management to Kafka brokers\n- Fetching records from assigned partitions\n- Offset management (position tracking and commits)\n- Consumer group coordination and rebalancing\n- Thread-safe wakeup signaling\n\n### Key Characteristics\n\n- **Not thread-safe**: All methods (except `wakeup()`) must be called from a single consumer thread\n- **Event-driven**: Uses a polling model; all coordination and network I/O occurs during `poll()`\n- **Group-managed**: Supports both automatic partition assignment via consumer groups and manual partition assignment\n- **Stateful**: Maintains position (offset) for each assigned partition\n\n### Threading Model\n\nThe Kafka consumer follows a **single-threaded event loop** model:\n- All consumer operations must occur on a single thread (the \"consumer thread\")\n- The `wakeup()` method is the **only thread-safe method** and can be safely called from any thread\n- Network communication, metadata updates, rebalancing callbacks, and offset commits all happen during `poll()` calls\n\n**Multi-threaded access without synchronization will result in `ConcurrentModificationException`.**\n\n---\n\n## Core Types\n\n### KafkaConsumer<K, V>\n\nThe main consumer class. Generic over key and value types.\n\n**Constructors:**\n\n```java\n// Map-based configuration\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n\n// Properties-based configuration\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties)\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\n\n### ConsumerRecord<K, V>\n\nRepresents a single record fetched from Kafka. Contains:\n\n```java\ntopic()                    // Topic name\npartition()                // Partition number\noffset()                   // Offset within partition\nkey()                      // Key (may be null)\nvalue()                    // Value payload\ntimestamp()                // Record timestamp\ntimestampType()            // Timestamp type (CreateTime or LogAppendTime)\nheaders()                  // Record headers\nserializedKeySize()        // Serialized key size in bytes\nserializedValueSize()      // Serialized value size in bytes\nleaderEpoch()              // Leader epoch (for log truncation detection)\ndeliveryCount()            // Delivery count (for retransmissions)\n```\n\n**Important:** `ConsumerRecord` is not thread-safe. Its mutable headers collection should not be accessed concurrently.\n\n### ConsumerRecords<K, V>\n\nBatch container for records. Returned by `poll()`.\n\n```java\n// Access methods\nList<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(TopicPartition partition)\nIterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(String topic)\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions()                    // Partitions with records\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsets() // Next offsets to fetch\nint count()                                         // Total record count\nboolean isEmpty()                                   // Check if empty\nIterator<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> iterator()          // Iterate all records\n```\n\n### OffsetAndMetadata\n\nRepresents an offset with optional metadata and leader epoch:\n\n```java\nlong offset()                          // Offset to commit\nString metadata()                      // User-provided metadata (empty string if none)\nOptional<Integer> leaderEpoch()        // Leader epoch for log truncation detection\n```\n\nConstructed with:\n```java\nnew OffsetAndMetadata(offset)                                    // Offset only\nnew OffsetAndMetadata(offset, metadata)                          // With metadata\nnew OffsetAndMetadata(offset, leaderEpoch, metadata)             // With leader epoch\n```\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener\n\nInterface for rebalancing callbacks. Invoked during `poll()` when partitions are reassigned.\n\n```java\ninterface ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    // Called when partitions are revoked (before rebalance completes)\n    void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n\n    // Called when partitions are assigned (after rebalance completes)\n    void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n\n    // Called when partitions are lost (exceptional scenarios)\n    default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        onPartitionsRevoked(partitions);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### OffsetAndTimestamp\n\nResult of timestamp-based offset lookup:\n\n```java\nlong timestamp()            // The matching timestamp\nlong offset()              // The offset with timestamp >= requested timestamp\n```\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Lifecycle\n\n### Construction\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n```\n\n**Important:** Resource cleanup is required. Always close the consumer in a finally block or use try-with-resources:\n\n```java\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (running) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        // Process records\n    }\n} // Consumer automatically closed\n```\n\n### Closing\n\nThe consumer should be closed gracefully to allow cleanup operations:\n\n```java\n// Default close (30 second timeout, default leave group behavior)\nconsumer.close();\n\n// Close with timeout\nconsumer.close(Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n\n// Close with options (control leave group behavior)\nconsumer.close(new CloseOptions().timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(10)));\n```\n\n**Cleanup operations performed:**\n1. Sends leave group request (depending on `CloseOptions.GroupMembershipOperation`)\n2. Commits offsets (if `enable.auto.commit=true`)\n3. Revokes rebalance listener partitions\n4. Closes network connections\n\n**Note:** The `wakeup()` method cannot interrupt `close()`.\n\n---\n\n## Subscription and Assignment\n\n### Subscribe (Group-Managed)\n\nDynamic partition assignment managed by Kafka broker:\n\n```java\n// Subscribe to specific topics\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"));\n\n// Subscribe with rebalance listener\nconsumer.subscribe(\n    Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"),\n    new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Commit offsets before losing partitions\n            consumer.commitSync();\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Initialize position for newly assigned partitions\n            for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n                long offset = getOffsetFromExternalStore(partition);\n                consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n);\n\n// Subscribe via regex\nPattern pattern = Pattern.compile(\"topic.*\");\nconsumer.subscribe(pattern);\nconsumer.subscribe(pattern, rebalanceListener);\n```\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n\n- **Non-incremental**: Each `subscribe()` call replaces the previous subscription\n- **Rebalances**: Automatic rebalance on topic count change, partition count change, or group membership change\n- **Callbacks timing**: Rebalance callbacks execute during `poll()` only\n- **Callback ordering**: `onPartitionsRevoked()` → `onPartitionsAssigned()` in normal scenarios\n- **Empty subscription**: Calling `subscribe(Collections.emptyList())` is equivalent to `unsubscribe()`\n\n### Assign (Manual Assignment)\n\nDirect partition assignment without group coordination:\n\n```java\nTopicPartition partition0 = new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 0);\nTopicPartition partition1 = new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 1);\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(partition0, partition1));\n```\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n\n- **No rebalancing**: Manual assignment bypasses group coordination\n- **No callbacks**: `ConsumerRebalanceListener` is not invoked\n- **Non-incremental**: Replaces previous assignment (manual or subscription)\n- **Use cases**:\n  - Specialized partition assignment logic\n  - Stateful processing (each consumer maintains local state per partition)\n  - Integration with external coordination systems\n- **Unique group ID**: Recommended to use unique `group.id` for each manually-assigned consumer to avoid offset conflicts\n\n### Unsubscribe\n\n```java\nconsumer.unsubscribe();\n```\n\nClears both subscriptions and manual assignments. Consumer has no partitions assigned after this call.\n\n### Subscription State\n\n```java\nSet<String> subscribed = consumer.subscription();      // Current topics (empty if using manual assign)\nSet<TopicPartition> assigned = consumer.assignment();  // Currently assigned partitions\n```\n\n---\n\n## Polling and Data Fetching\n\n### poll(Duration timeout)\n\nFetches records from assigned partitions. **Central operation** in the consumer loop.\n\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\nfor (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n    System.out.println(\"Topic: \" + record.topic() +\n                      \", Partition: \" + record.partition() +\n                      \", Offset: \" + record.offset() +\n                      \", Key: \" + record.key() +\n                      \", Value: \" + record.value());\n}\n```\n\n**Blocking Behavior:**\n\n- Returns immediately if records are available\n- Returns immediately if position advances past control records or aborted transactions (read_committed)\n- Waits up to timeout if no records available and no immediate triggers\n- **May block longer than timeout** if:\n  - Rebalancing is in progress\n  - Rebalance callbacks are executing\n  - Network metadata refresh is needed\n  - Broker is unavailable\n\n**Behavior Semantics:**\n\n| Scenario | Behavior |\n|----------|----------|\n| Records available | Returns immediately with records |\n| No records, normal case | Waits up to timeout, returns empty |\n| Rebalance triggered | Executes callbacks (may exceed timeout) |\n| Metadata needs refresh | Fetches metadata before returning |\n| Consumer paused | Returns immediately (empty) |\n| Position invalid | Applies `auto.offset.reset` policy |\n\n**Automatic Offset Commits:**\n\nIf `enable.auto.commit=true`:\n- Offsets are committed periodically during `poll()` (interval controlled by `auto.commit.interval.ms`)\n- Commits the last **position** returned from previous `poll()` calls\n- Failures are logged but not thrown\n\n**What Happens During poll():**\n\n1. Update metadata if needed\n2. Check for session timeout / max.poll.interval.ms violations\n3. Execute rebalance callbacks if rebalancing\n4. Refresh committed offsets on assignment\n5. Fetch records from brokers\n6. Deserialize records (may throw `RecordDeserializationException`)\n7. Filter control records and aborted transactional messages (if `read_committed`)\n8. Commit offsets (if auto-commit enabled)\n9. Return `ConsumerRecords`\n\n**Exceptions Thrown:**\n\n- `WakeupException`: If `wakeup()` was called\n- `InterruptException`: If thread was interrupted\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: Position undefined or out of range\n- `RecordDeserializationException`: Deserialization failed\n- `AuthenticationException`: Authentication failed\n- `AuthorizationException`: Not authorized\n- `KafkaException`: Other unrecoverable errors\n\n---\n\n## Offset Management\n\n### Offset Concepts\n\nThree offset concepts are important:\n\n1. **Position**: The offset of the next record to be fetched\n   - Maintained by consumer\n   - Advances on each `poll()` call\n   - Controlled via `seek()` operations\n   - Not persisted; lost on restart\n\n2. **Committed Offset**: The last offset successfully committed\n   - Persisted in Kafka or external store\n   - Used to resume after restart\n   - Must always be the **next offset to read** (position + already-processed)\n   - Accessed via `committed()`\n\n3. **Offset Lag**: Position - Committed\n   - Distance between what's been read and what's been committed\n   - Indicates potential data loss on failure\n\n### Auto-commit\n\nOffsets committed automatically if `enable.auto.commit=true`:\n\n```properties\nenable.auto.commit=true\nauto.commit.interval.ms=5000  # Commit every 5 seconds\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n- Commits during `poll()` at configured interval\n- Commits the position (next offset to read)\n- Failures are logged, not thrown\n- With `enable.auto.commit=true`, you **must** consume all records returned by `poll()` or risk skipping records\n\n**When NOT to use auto-commit:**\n- Processing time is unpredictable\n- Need exactly-once semantics\n- Processing result must be atomic with offset commit\n- Using external offset storage\n\n### Manual Synchronous Commit\n\n```java\n// Commit all offsets\nconsumer.commitSync();\n\n// Commit with timeout\nconsumer.commitSync(Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n\n// Commit specific offsets\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    offsets.put(partition, records.nextOffsets().get(partition));\n}\nconsumer.commitSync(offsets);\n\n// Commit per-partition\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    long nextOffset = records.records(partition).isEmpty()\n        ? consumer.position(partition)\n        : records.records(partition).get(records.records(partition).size() - 1).offset() + 1;\n    consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n        partition,\n        new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset)\n    ));\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- **Blocks** until commit completes or timeout\n- **Retries** retriable errors automatically\n- Throws `CommitFailedException` if partitions are lost (group rebalanced)\n- Throws `TimeoutException` if timeout expires\n\n**When to use:**\n- After successfully processing and persisting records\n- In rebalance listener `onPartitionsRevoked()`\n- Before closing consumer\n\n### Manual Asynchronous Commit\n\n```java\n// Fire and forget\nconsumer.commitAsync();\n\n// With callback\nconsumer.commitAsync((offsets, exception) -> {\n    if (exception != null) {\n        logger.error(\"Commit failed: \" + exception);\n        // Handle error (may need to retry or shutdown)\n    } else {\n        logger.info(\"Offsets committed: \" + offsets);\n    }\n});\n\n// Commit specific offsets with callback\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    offsets.put(partition, records.nextOffsets().get(partition));\n}\nconsumer.commitAsync(offsets, callback);\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- **Non-blocking** - returns immediately\n- Callback executes asynchronously\n- Multiple async commits maintain order\n- Async commits complete before subsequent `commitSync()`\n- Failures in callback are handled by callback only (not thrown)\n\n**Common Pattern:**\n```java\nconsumer.commitAsync((offsets, exception) -> {\n    if (exception != null) {\n        // Log but continue (retry on next success)\n    }\n});\n```\n\n### Commit Failure Scenarios\n\n**CommitFailedException:**\n- Consumer is no longer part of group\n- Rebalance occurred before commit completed\n- `max.poll.interval.ms` exceeded\n- Session timed out\n\n**Recovery:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Partitions likely reassigned; cannot retry\n    // Shutdown cleanly or let next poll() discover new assignment\n    logger.error(\"Commit failed, consumer out of group\", e);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Position and Seek Operations\n\n### Getting Position\n\n```java\n// Next offset that will be fetched\nlong position = consumer.position(partition);\n\n// With timeout\nlong position = consumer.position(partition, Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Returns offset of next record to be fetched\n- May trigger remote call to broker if not yet determined\n- Throws `InvalidOffsetException` if undefined\n- Blocks up to timeout\n\n### Seeking to Offsets\n\n```java\n// Seek to specific offset\nconsumer.seek(partition, 100L);\n\n// Seek to beginning\nconsumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singleton(partition));\nconsumer.seekToBeginning();  // All assigned partitions\n\n// Seek to end\nconsumer.seekToEnd(Collections.singleton(partition));\nconsumer.seekToEnd();  // All assigned partitions\n\n// Seek with leader epoch (for log truncation detection)\nconsumer.seek(partition, new OffsetAndMetadata(100L, Optional.of(5)));\n```\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n\n- **Lazy evaluation**: Seek changes don't take effect until next `poll()`\n- **In-flight requests**: Existing fetch requests complete before new position takes effect\n- **Invalid offset handling**: Controlled by `auto.offset.reset` policy:\n  - `earliest`: Seek to beginning\n  - `latest`: Seek to end\n  - `none`: Throw `OffsetOutOfRangeException`\n- **seekToEnd for read_committed**: Seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO), not high watermark\n- **Position after seek**: Call `position()` after `poll()` to see actual position\n\n### Seeking by Timestamp\n\n```java\n// Find offsets for given timestamps\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch = new HashMap<>();\ntimestampsToSearch.put(partition1, System.currentTimeMillis() - 60000); // 1 min ago\ntimestampsToSearch.put(partition2, System.currentTimeMillis());\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> results = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestampsToSearch);\n\nfor (TopicPartition partition : results.keySet()) {\n    OffsetAndTimestamp result = results.get(partition);\n    if (result != null) {\n        consumer.seek(partition, result.offset());\n    } else {\n        // No message found for timestamp\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n- Returns earliest offset with timestamp >= requested timestamp\n- Returns `null` if no matching offset or topic has no timestamps\n- Requires message format v0.10+\n- Blocks up to timeout\n\n### Beginning and End Offsets\n\n```java\n// First available offset\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginnings = consumer.beginningOffsets(partitions);\n\n// Last offset\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> ends = consumer.endOffsets(partitions);\n```\n\n**Semantics:**\n\n- **Beginning**: First offset in partition (log start offset)\n- **End**: One past last offset\n  - For `read_uncommitted`: High watermark\n  - For `read_committed`: Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Does not change consumer position\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Groups and Rebalancing\n\n### Group Coordination\n\nKafka consumer groups provide automatic partition assignment and failure detection:\n\n**How it works:**\n1. Consumer joins group on first `poll()`\n2. Broker detects membership changes\n3. Broker triggers rebalance\n4. Members execute `onPartitionsRevoked()` callbacks\n5. Broker assigns new partitions\n6. Members execute `onPartitionsAssigned()` callbacks\n7. Normal consumption resumes\n\n### Rebalance Triggers\n\nRebalances occur when:\n- New consumer joins group\n- Consumer leaves/crashes\n- Subscribed topics change partition count\n- New topics match subscription pattern\n- Manually triggered via `enforceRebalance()`\n\n### Rebalance Listeners\n\nImplement `ConsumerRebalanceListener` for custom logic:\n\n```java\nclass RebalanceListener implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Called when losing partitions (before reassignment)\n        // - Commit offsets\n        // - Flush writes\n        // - Release resources\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Called after new assignment (before fetching)\n        // - Initialize position\n        // - Load state\n        // - Open resources\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = readOffsetFromExternalStore(partition);\n            consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Called when partitions unexpectedly lost (e.g., timeout)\n        // Partitions may already be owned by other consumers\n        // - Don't commit (might fail)\n        // - Clean up resources\n        // - Default: delegates to onPartitionsRevoked()\n    }\n}\n\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"), new RebalanceListener());\n```\n\n**Callback Execution:**\n- Callbacks execute during `poll()` only\n- On rebalance, `poll()` may block longer than timeout\n- Exceptions in callbacks propagate to caller of `poll()`\n- `WakeupException` or `InterruptException` from callbacks propagate to `poll()`\n\n### Rebalance Protocols\n\nKafka supports two rebalancing protocols:\n\n**Classic (Eager) Rebalancing:**\n- All members stop consuming\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called with ALL partitions\n- Broker assigns partitions\n- `onPartitionsAssigned()` called with all partitions (even unchanged)\n- Higher downtime, simpler logic\n\n**Cooperative Rebalancing:**\n- Members retain partitions when possible\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called only with revoked partitions\n- Broker assigns partitions\n- `onPartitionsAssigned()` called only with new partitions\n- Lower downtime, more complex\n\nControl via `partition.assignment.strategy`:\n```properties\npartition.assignment.strategy=org.apache.kafka.clients.consumer.CooperativeStickyAssignor\n```\n\n### Heartbeat and Session Management\n\n```properties\nsession.timeout.ms=10000        # Seconds without heartbeat before removal\nmax.poll.interval.ms=300000     # Max time between polls (liveness check)\nheartbeat.interval.ms=3000      # Heartbeat frequency\n```\n\n**Session Timeout:**\n- If consumer can't send heartbeat for `session.timeout.ms`, broker removes it\n- Other members trigger rebalance\n- Consumer unaware until next `poll()`\n\n**Max Poll Interval:**\n- If consumer doesn't call `poll()` within `max.poll.interval.ms`, proactively leaves group\n- Prevents consumer from holding partitions while hung\n- Next `poll()` triggers rebalance\n- Subsequent `commitSync()` throws `CommitFailedException`\n\n### Force Rebalance\n\n```java\n// Non-blocking; rebalance occurs on next poll()\nconsumer.enforceRebalance();\nconsumer.enforceRebalance(\"user-initiated rebalance\");\n```\n\nUse case: When external state (not tracked by Kafka) changes and requires partition reassignment.\n\n### Group Metadata\n\n```java\nConsumerGroupMetadata metadata = consumer.groupMetadata();\n// Contains: group ID, member ID, generation\n```\n\nUsed when manually coordinating with transactional producers.\n\n---\n\n## Flow Control\n\n### Pause and Resume\n\nControl which partitions are fetched:\n\n```java\n// Pause (no records returned for these partitions)\nconsumer.pause(Arrays.asList(partition1, partition2));\n\n// Resume\nconsumer.resume(Arrays.asList(partition1, partition2));\n\n// Check paused partitions\nSet<TopicPartition> paused = consumer.paused();\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- Slow consumers: Pause fast partitions while processing slow ones\n- Stream join: Pause ahead stream while lagging stream catches up\n- Backpressure: Pause while downstream queue is full\n- Batching: Pause some partitions to batch process others\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n- Pause doesn't affect subscription or assignment\n- Does not trigger rebalance\n- Rebalance does NOT preserve pause/resume state\n- Call `pause()` again after rebalance if needed\n\n### Pattern: Controlled Processing\n\n```java\nwhile (running) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n    // Process with pause/resume for flow control\n    processingQueue.addAll(records);\n\n    if (processingQueue.size() > 10000) {\n        // Too many pending; pause faster partitions\n        Set<TopicPartition> fastPartitions = identifyFastPartitions();\n        consumer.pause(fastPartitions);\n    } else if (processingQueue.size() < 1000) {\n        // Queue emptying; resume\n        consumer.resume(paused);\n    }\n\n    processQueue();\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Metadata and Partition Information\n\n### Partition Information\n\n```java\nList<PartitionInfo> partitions = consumer.partitionsFor(\"topic\");\n// Returns: List of PartitionInfo (partition #, leader, replicas, in-sync replicas)\n```\n\n### List All Topics\n\n```java\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> allTopics = consumer.listTopics();\n// All topics consumer is authorized to access\n```\n\n### Current Lag\n\n```java\nOptionalLong lag = consumer.currentLag(partition);\n// Returns: position - end offset (or empty if unknown)\n```\n\n### Metrics\n\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics = consumer.metrics();\n// Includes: record lag, fetch latency, bytes consumed, etc.\n```\n\n---\n\n## Multi-threaded Processing\n\n### Thread Safety\n\n**KafkaConsumer is NOT thread-safe.**\n\nOnly the `wakeup()` method is thread-safe and can be called from any thread.\n\n### Pattern 1: One Consumer Per Thread\n\nSimplest approach. Each thread has its own consumer:\n\n```java\nExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(4);\n\nfor (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {\n    executor.submit(() -> {\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n            while (running.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    processRecord(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    });\n}\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- Simplest implementation\n- No inter-thread synchronization\n- In-order processing per partition guaranteed\n\n**Cons:**\n- More TCP connections\n- Limited by partition count\n- Cannot scale beyond partition count\n\n### Pattern 2: Consumer + Processing Thread Pool\n\nOne consumer thread feeds work queue to processors:\n\n```java\nclass ConsumerRunner implements Runnable {\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n    private final BlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue;\n    private final AtomicBoolean running;\n\n    @Override\n    public void run() {\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n            while (running.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    try {\n                        queue.put(record);  // Blocks if queue full\n                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                // Pause if queue too full\n                if (queue.size() > 10000) {\n                    consumer.pause(consumer.assignment());\n                } else if (queue.size() < 1000 && paused) {\n                    consumer.resume(consumer.assignment());\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Processing threads\nfor (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {\n    executor.submit(() -> {\n        while (running.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.take();\n            processRecord(record);\n            offsetsToCommit.put(record.partition(), record.offset() + 1);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n// Periodic commit thread\nexecutor.submit(() -> {\n    while (running.get()) {\n        Thread.sleep(5000);\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\n        offsetsToCommit.forEach((partition, offset) ->\n            offsets.put(partition, new OffsetAndMetadata(offset))\n        );\n        consumer.commitAsync(offsets);\n    }\n});\n```\n\n**Pros:**\n- Scales beyond partition count\n- Can process independently\n- Flexible throughput tuning\n\n**Cons:**\n- Complex offset management\n- Lost message ordering guarantees\n- Potential for duplicate processing\n\n### Shutting Down\n\n```java\nExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(2);\n\n// Consumer thread\nFuture<?> consumerFuture = executor.submit(consumerRunnable);\n\n// Shutdown\nrunning.set(false);\nexecutor.awaitTermination(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n\nif (!executor.isTerminated()) {\n    executor.shutdownNow();\n}\n```\n\n### Wakeup Pattern\n\nInterrupt blocking operations from another thread:\n\n```java\n// Consumer thread\ntry {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (running.get()) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n        processRecords(records);\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    if (!running.get()) {\n        // Expected shutdown\n    } else {\n        throw e;\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n\n// Shutdown thread\npublic void shutdown() {\n    running.set(false);\n    consumer.wakeup();  // Safe to call from any thread\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Exception Hierarchy\n\n```\nKafkaException (base)\n├── WakeupException (from wakeup())\n├── InterruptException (from thread interruption)\n├── AuthenticationException (auth failed)\n├── AuthorizationException (not authorized)\n├── TimeoutException (operation timed out)\n├── CommitFailedException (can't commit, out of group)\n├── RetriableCommitFailedException (commit may succeed if retried)\n├── InvalidOffsetException (position undefined/out of range)\n├── NoOffsetForPartitionException (no offset found)\n├── OffsetOutOfRangeException (auto.offset.reset=none)\n├── LogTruncationException (committed offset lost to log truncation)\n├── RecordDeserializationException (deserialization failed)\n├── InvalidGroupIdException (bad group ID)\n└── ... (others)\n```\n\n### WakeupException\n\nRaised when `wakeup()` was called:\n\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    // wakeup() was called; clean up and exit\n    break;\n}\n```\n\n### CommitFailedException\n\nRaised when commit fails due to group rebalancing:\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Consumer no longer in group\n    // Cannot commit; partitions reassigned\n    // Solution: Retry on next poll() or shutdown\n    logger.error(\"Commit failed, out of group\", e);\n}\n```\n\n### InvalidOffsetException\n\nPosition is invalid (outside log bounds):\n\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (InvalidOffsetException e) {\n    // Position undefined or out of range\n    // auto.offset.reset policy applies on next poll()\n    // Or seek explicitly: consumer.seek(partition, validOffset);\n}\n```\n\n### RecordDeserializationException\n\nDeserialization failed for a record:\n\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (RecordDeserializationException e) {\n    // Record deserialization failed\n    // Partition: e.topicPartition()\n    // Offset: e.offset()\n    // Solution: skip record or shutdown\n\n    // Skip to next record\n    consumer.seek(e.topicPartition(), e.offset() + 1);\n}\n```\n\n### AuthenticationException / AuthorizationException\n\nAuthentication or authorization failed:\n\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n    // Invalid credentials\n    logger.error(\"Authentication failed\", e);\n} catch (AuthorizationException e) {\n    // Not authorized to read topic/group\n    logger.error(\"Not authorized\", e);\n}\n```\n\n### Common Error Handling Patterns\n\n**Pattern 1: Log and Retry**\n```java\nwhile (true) {\n    try {\n        consumer.commitSync();\n        break;\n    } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n        logger.warn(\"Commit failed, retrying\", e);\n        Thread.sleep(100);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Pattern 2: Log and Fail**\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    processRecords(records);\n} catch (KafkaException e) {\n    logger.error(\"Fatal error\", e);\n    System.exit(1);\n}\n```\n\n**Pattern 3: Skip Bad Records**\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (ConsumerRecord record : records) {\n        try {\n            processRecord(record);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.error(\"Failed to process record at offset \" + record.offset(), e);\n            // Continue with next record\n        }\n    }\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    // Shutdown\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Configuration-Driven Behaviors\n\n### Key Configuration Properties\n\n| Property | Default | Impact |\n|----------|---------|--------|\n| `bootstrap.servers` | (required) | Initial brokers to connect |\n| `group.id` | (required) | Consumer group ID |\n| `key.deserializer` | (required) | Key deserializer class |\n| `value.deserializer` | (required) | Value deserializer class |\n| `enable.auto.commit` | true | Auto-commit offsets |\n| `auto.commit.interval.ms` | 5000 | Commit interval |\n| `session.timeout.ms` | 10000 | Heartbeat timeout |\n| `max.poll.interval.ms` | 300000 | Max time between polls |\n| `max.poll.records` | 500 | Max records per poll |\n| `auto.offset.reset` | latest | Position policy (earliest/latest/none) |\n| `isolation.level` | read_uncommitted | Transactional semantics |\n| `fetch.min.bytes` | 1 | Min bytes to return |\n| `fetch.max.wait.ms` | 500 | Max wait for min bytes |\n| `fetch.max.bytes` | 52428800 | Max bytes per fetch |\n| `default.api.timeout.ms` | 60000 | Default timeout |\n| `partition.assignment.strategy` | RangeAssignor | Assignment algorithm |\n\n### Auto-commit Behavior\n\nWith `enable.auto.commit=true`:\n- Offsets committed automatically during `poll()`\n- Interval controlled by `auto.commit.interval.ms`\n- Commits the latest position\n- Failures logged, not thrown\n\n**Risk:** If `poll()` returns records but they're not processed before the next `poll()` or `close()`, records are skipped.\n\n**Solution:** Disable auto-commit if processing time is significant:\n```properties\nenable.auto.commit=false\n```\n\n### Offset Reset Policy\n\nWhen position is invalid (out of range):\n\n- `earliest`: Seek to beginning of partition\n- `latest`: Seek to end of partition\n- `none`: Throw `OffsetOutOfRangeException`\n\n**Triggered by:**\n- Committed offset lost to log compaction or retention\n- Manual seek to invalid offset\n- `auto.offset.reset` applies on next `poll()`\n\n### Isolation Level\n\n**`read_uncommitted` (default):**\n- Reads all messages\n- Includes aborted transactional messages\n- End offset = high watermark\n\n**`read_committed`:**\n- Skips aborted transactional messages\n- End offset = Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- No client-side buffering\n- Slower due to LSO computation\n\n### Poll Timeout Behavior\n\n`max.poll.records` limits batch size:\n```properties\nmax.poll.records=100  # Return max 100 records\n```\n\nLarge batches require more time to process. If processing time exceeds `max.poll.interval.ms`, consumer is removed from group.\n\n**Tuning:**\n- Reduce `max.poll.records` if processing is slow\n- Or increase `max.poll.interval.ms` (impact: slower rebalance detection)\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Basic Consumption with Auto-commit\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"true\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.println(\"Key: \" + record.key() + \", Value: \" + record.value());\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Best for:** Simple log consumption, high throughput, at-least-once acceptable.\n\n### Pattern 2: Exactly-Once with Manual Commit\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        try {\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                saveToDatabase(record);  // Atomic with offset in transaction\n            }\n            consumer.commitSync();  // Commit only after successful save\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            logger.error(\"Processing failed, will retry\", e);\n            // Don't commit; next poll() will re-fetch\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Best for:** Transactional processing, databases, at-least-once guarantees.\n\n### Pattern 3: External Offset Management with Rebalance Listener\n\n```java\nConsumerRebalanceListener listener = new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Commit last processed offset to external store\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = lastProcessedOffset.get(partition);\n            externalStore.saveOffset(partition, offset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Load offsets from external store\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = externalStore.getOffset(partition);\n            consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"), listener);\n\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        processAndStore(record);\n        lastProcessedOffset.put(record.partition(), record.offset() + 1);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Best for:** Exactly-once with external state storage, stream processing.\n\n### Pattern 4: Processing with Thread Pool\n\n```java\nBlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(10000);\nAtomicBoolean running = new AtomicBoolean(true);\n\n// Consumer thread\nexecutor.submit(() -> {\n    try (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n        while (running.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                queue.put(record);\n            }\n\n            // Flow control\n            if (queue.size() > 8000) {\n                consumer.pause(consumer.assignment());\n            } else if (queue.size() < 2000 && !consumer.paused().isEmpty()) {\n                consumer.resume(consumer.paused());\n            }\n        }\n    }\n});\n\n// Processing threads\nfor (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {\n    executor.submit(() -> {\n        while (running.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.take();\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n// Graceful shutdown\nRuntime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(() -> {\n    running.set(false);\n    executor.awaitTermination(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n}));\n```\n\n**Best for:** High-throughput processing, independent task processing, scaling.\n\n### Pattern 5: Handling Deserialization Errors\n\n```java\nwhile (true) {\n    try {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            try {\n                processRecord(record);\n                lastGoodOffset.put(record.partition(), record.offset() + 1);\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                logger.error(\"Failed to process record\", e);\n                // Log and continue\n            }\n        }\n    } catch (RecordDeserializationException e) {\n        logger.error(\"Deserialization failed at offset \" + e.offset(), e);\n        // Skip bad record\n        consumer.seek(e.topicPartition(), e.offset() + 1);\n    } catch (WakeupException e) {\n        break;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Best Practices\n\n1. **Always close the consumer** to release resources and leave group gracefully\n2. **Use manual commit for important data** to ensure exactly-once semantics\n3. **Implement ConsumerRebalanceListener** when using manual offsets or external state\n4. **Set `max.poll.interval.ms` appropriately** for your processing time\n5. **Prefer `commitSync()` in rebalance callbacks** to ensure commit before losing partitions\n6. **Use pause/resume for flow control** instead of stopping the poll loop\n7. **Handle `CommitFailedException`** as unrecoverable; let next poll discover new assignment\n8. **Log and skip bad records** rather than crashing on deserialization errors\n9. **Monitor consumer lag** for performance tuning\n10. **Test graceful shutdown** with `wakeup()` + `close()`\n\n### Offset Commit Best Practices\n\n| Requirement | Strategy |\n|-------------|----------|\n| High throughput, at-least-once | Auto-commit |\n| Exactly-once, databases | Manual sync commit after successful persist |\n| Stream processing, state store | ConsumerRebalanceListener + manual commits |\n| External offset storage | Rebalance listener callbacks |\n| Exactly-once with producer | Transactional read + write with `isolation.level=read_committed` |\n\n---\n\n## Transactional Message Consumption\n\nWhen consuming transactional producer writes:\n\n```properties\nisolation.level=read_committed\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Only reads committed transactional messages\n- Skips aborted messages (no client-side filtering)\n- End offset = Last Stable Offset (first offset of open transaction)\n- `seekToEnd()` seeks to LSO, not high watermark\n- Slightly higher latency than `read_uncommitted`\n\n**Use case:** Exactly-once stream processing where input and output are both transactional.\n\n---\n\n## Example: Complete Application\n\n```java\npublic class KafkaConsumerApp {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n        props.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n        props.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\n        props.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n        props.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\n        props.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\n        props.setProperty(\"max.poll.records\", \"100\");\n        props.setProperty(\"session.timeout.ms\", \"30000\");\n        props.setProperty(\"max.poll.interval.ms\", \"600000\");\n\n        KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        AtomicBoolean running = new AtomicBoolean(true);\n\n        // Rebalance listener\n        consumer.subscribe(\n            Arrays.asList(\"orders\", \"payments\"),\n            new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n                @Override\n                public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n                    logger.info(\"Revoking partitions: {}\", partitions);\n                    consumer.commitSync();  // Ensure offset committed\n                }\n\n                @Override\n                public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n                    logger.info(\"Assigning partitions: {}\", partitions);\n                    // Initialize position (default: use committed offset)\n                }\n            }\n        );\n\n        // Shutdown hook\n        Runtime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(() -> {\n            logger.info(\"Shutdown signal received\");\n            running.set(false);\n            consumer.wakeup();\n        }));\n\n        // Main loop\n        try {\n            while (running.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n\n                int count = 0;\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    try {\n                        handleRecord(record);\n                        count++;\n                    } catch (Exception e) {\n                        logger.error(\"Failed to process record at offset {}\", record.offset(), e);\n                        // Continue with next record\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (count > 0) {\n                    try {\n                        consumer.commitSync(Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n                        logger.info(\"Committed {} records\", count);\n                    } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n                        logger.error(\"Commit failed, will shutdown\", e);\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            logger.info(\"Consumer woken up\");\n        } finally {\n            try {\n                consumer.commitSync();\n                logger.info(\"Final commit completed\");\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                logger.error(\"Final commit failed\", e);\n            }\n            consumer.close();\n            logger.info(\"Consumer closed\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void handleRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        // Business logic\n        System.out.println(\"Processing: \" + record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe Kafka `KafkaConsumer` API provides:\n\n- **Simple polling interface** for record consumption\n- **Automatic group management** with configurable assignment strategies\n- **Flexible offset management** (auto or manual, sync or async)\n- **Rebalance callbacks** for state management during group changes\n- **Flow control** via pause/resume for backpressure\n- **Rich metadata queries** for partition and offset information\n- **Thread-safe wakeup** for coordinated shutdown\n- **Comprehensive error handling** with specific exception types\n\nMaster the offset semantics, rebalance callbacks, and polling behavior for reliable Kafka
